***rookwaar.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:rookwaar.html>rookwaar</a> (79928)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:roken.html>roken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to smoke</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>waar</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:ware.html>ware</a>, product</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rookwaar.html>rookwaar</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rookwaren.html>rookwaren</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">collective</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> smoking products <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">tobacco products, sometimes including other smoked <a href = vnd.unilang:drugs.html>drugs</a> and smoking miscellanea</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:roosteren.html>roosteren</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">roostre</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">roester</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fire-grate, <a href = vnd.unilang:toaster.html>toaster</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">rôsteren</i>.
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ros.html>ros</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:ros.html>ros</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:hors.html>hors</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hrussą</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">horse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱers-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to run</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kar.html>kar</a></i>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***rosemary.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:rosemary.html>rosemary</a> (10755)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:rose.html>rose</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mary.html>Mary</a></i>. From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">rosmary</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">rosemarye</i>, alteration (based on <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:rose.html>rose</a></i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:mary.html>Mary</a></i>) of earlier <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">rosmarine</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">rosemaryn</i>, partly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">rosmarin</i>, partly directly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">rōsmarīnus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:rosemary.html>rosemary</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">rōs</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dew, moisture</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">marīnus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">marine, of the sea</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:rosemary.html>rosemary</a></strong> (<i>usually uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">rosemaries</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A shrub, <i>Rosmarinus officinalis</i>, that originates from Europe and Asia Minor and produces a fragrant herb used in cooking and perfumes.</li></ol>

***rossen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:rossen.html>rossen</a> (59376)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rossen.html>rossen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To beat, to rough up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beste.html>beste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vriend.html>vriend</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gisteren.html>gisteren</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:rossen.html>gerost</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ploertendoder.html>ploertendoders</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">They <b>beat up</b> my <a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a> friend with <a href = vnd.unilang:blackjacks.html>blackjacks</a> yesterday.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:rotonde.html>rotonde</a> (30961)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:rotonde.html>rotonde</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">rotonda</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">rotondus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rotonde.html>rotonde</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rotondes.html>rotondes</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">rotonden</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rotonde.html>rotondetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A roundabout (road junction at which traffic <a href = vnd.unilang:streams.html>streams</a> circularly around a central island). <span class="defdate">[from ca. 1940]</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">rondpunt</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">verkeersplein</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <span class="Latn" lang="en">rotunda</span>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A sleeveless coat worn by women.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:rotsachtig.html>rotsachtig</a> (79908)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rots.html>rots</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-achtig</i>.

***rotzak.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:rotzak.html>rotzak</a> (2684)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rot.html>rot</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:rotten.html>rotten</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zak.html>zak</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:scrotum.html>scrotum</a>, bag</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Reportedly (WNT, <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vries.html>Vries</a>) a bahuvrihi meaning “a syphilitic”. Syphilis <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> also known as the French disease, explaining why it became a slur for French and Walloon people.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rotzak.html>rotzak</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rotzakken.html>rotzakken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rotzak.html>rotzakje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:scumbag.html>scumbag</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:fiend.html>fiend</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belgium" class="extiw" title="w:Belgium">Belgium</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Brabant" class="extiw" title="w:Brabant">Brabant</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">Eurasian <a href = vnd.unilang:jay.html>jay</a></span>, <i>Garrulus glandarius</i>
<ul><li><b>1966</b>, Gerard Walschap, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> Gastmaal</i>, page 123.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>Zij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hielden.html>hielden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lucht.html>lucht</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oog.html>oog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tegen.html>tegen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:roofvogels.html>roofvogels</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:rotzakken.html>rotzakken</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:alias.html>alias</a> vlaamse <a href = vnd.unilang:gaaien.html>gaaien</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:spraken.html>spraken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nieuws.html>nieuws</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:problemen.html>problemen</a>.</span><dl><dd><small>(please add an English translation of this quote)</small></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:rotzak.html>rotzak</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:rouw.html>rouw</a> (9342)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:rouwen.html>rouwe</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruwe.html>ruwe</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*reuwa</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hrewwōn</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hrewwō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pain, sadness, regret, repentance</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">hrēow</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">rue</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Reue</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">hryggr</i>. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en">rue</span>. The noun <i><a href = vnd.unilang:rouw.html>rouw</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:belongs.html>belongs</a> to the verb <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rouwen.html>rouwen</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:rozemarijn.html>rozemarijn</a> (23701)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">rosmarin</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">rosmarin</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">rōs marīnus</i>. Secondarily influenced by <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:roos.html>roos</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:rose.html>rose</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, for which compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:rosemary.html>rosemary</a></i>.
</p>

***rozenkrans.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:rozenkrans.html>rozenkrans</a> (16480)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">rosencrans</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:roos.html>roos</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:rose.html>rose</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:krans.html>krans</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wreath</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rozenkrans.html>rozenkrans</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rozenkransen.html>rozenkransen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rozenkrans.html>rozenkransje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <span class="Latn" lang="en">wreath</span> of <span class="Latn" lang="en">roses</span></li>
<li>The <span class="Latn" lang="en">rosary</span>, a Catholic <span class="Latn" lang="en">prayer</span> sequence, consisting of repetitions of <span class="Latn" lang="en">Our Lady</span> and <span class="Latn" lang="en">Our Father</span></li>
<li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en">rosary</span>, Catholic or, less commonly, Anglican <span class="Latn" lang="en">prayer beads</span> used to keep track of the above</li>
<li>An object resembling the wreath:
<ol><li>a deer's <span class="Latn" lang="en">antlers</span>' <span class="Latn" lang="en">knobby</span> edges</li>
<li>the plant <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Gnaphalium_dioicum" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Gnaphalium dioicum"><i>Gnaphalium dioicum</i></a></span>, now <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Antennaria_dioica" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Antennaria dioica"><i>Antennaria dioica</i></a></span></li></ol></li>
<li>A symbolical meaning of the wreath:
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">youth</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">virginity</span></li></ol></li></ol>

***rubriek.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:rubriek.html>rubriek</a> (31608)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">rubrike</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">red pigment</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">rubrique</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">rubrīca</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">red ochre</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the substance used to make red <a href = vnd.unilang:letters.html>letters</a>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruber.html>ruber</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">red</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₁rewdʰ-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rubriek.html>rubriek</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rubrieken.html>rubrieken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rubriek.html>rubriekje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">rubric</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">header</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a title, header or written character, in particular one written in red</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> red pigment</li></ol>

***rudd.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:rudd.html>rudd</a> (53345)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:rudd.html>rudd</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">rudds</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:rudd.html>rudd</a></strong></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any species of the freshwater game <a href = vnd.unilang:fishes.html>fishes</a> of genus <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Scardinius" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Scardinius"><i>Scardinius</i></a></span>
<ol><li><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/common_rudd" class="extiw" title="w:common rudd">common <a href = vnd.unilang:rudd.html>rudd</a></a> (<i><span class="Latn" lang="mul">Scardinius erythrophthalmus</span></i>)</li></ol>
<ul><li><b>2007</b>, Martin James, "<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/lancashire/content/articles/2007/06/15/fishing_martin_james_2007_season.shtml">At the Waters Edge blog!</a>," <i>BBC <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> Lancashire <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> Sport</i> (retrieved 2 Aug 2010):
<dl><dd>Within minutes of starting I <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> my first fish a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:rudd.html>rudd</a></b> about a pound, this <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> followed by a tench about five pounds.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
